            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                
    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
            <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">
        </i>

        11/30/2015

                <div class="review_tags">
                
        <span  class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i  class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite"></i> 1 check-in</span>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Really interesting restaurant, mainly opened for Business People around the area (they don&#39;t open in weekends). Here is one of those places that makes me want to go work at Downtown.<br><br>American and Fusion style food, taste is delicious, well known for their burgers which taste good, a bit oily on my preference, but overall really nice quality, quantity and presentation. It worth to try.<br><br>What blew my mind wasn&#39;t the burger tho... It was the special of the day - Leek Soup, that is one of the best soups I have ever tried.<br><br>The place is worth to visit, get together with friends, have some drinks or coffee. The staff is really friendly and customer caring.<br><br>BTW, at the beginning is hard to find the place since there are constructions around, so take your time and the delicious food will pay back :D<br><br>Good luck with your visit!</p>

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                
    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_3" title="3.0 star rating">
            <img alt="3.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3.0">
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-11-17">
        11/17/2015
    </span>

    </div>

        
                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Had dinner here on a Tuesday at 5:30pm before a Leafs game but I wasn&#39;t too impressed.<br><br>Seating is pretty limited, as it&#39;s a fairly small place.  The atmosphere was that of a casual but upscale bar.  Unfortunately, my table and dining space was so small, I was almost bumping elbows with the person beside me.<br><br>I got the chicken pot pie but had to wait about 25 min.  I will admit that it was worth the wait because it was delicious!  It&#39;s pretty heavy but so very creamy and full of flavour.  The chicken was incredibly moist and the pastry was flaky and delicious.  I was a bit disappointed that it doesn&#39;t come with any sides but it was filling enough for a dinner.<br><br>The big con was the price.  The chicken pot pie was $20 and a can of Coke was $4.  I wanted to get the soup as well but was not going to pay $9 for it.<br><br>Overall, I had a delicious dinner but felt I paid too much for what I got, and I had to rub elbows with my neighbour.</p> 
            
    </div>

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                
    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
            <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5.0">
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-11-14">
        11/14/2015
    </span>

    </div>

                <div class="review_tags">
                
        <span  class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i  class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite"></i> 2 check-ins</span>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Found this gem when i was searching for a nearby western restaurant close to work with good food on yelp and I am glad I had the opportunity to come here.  This place is a small little restaurant with a bar table near the door, it has tables that can fit around 30 people at a time.  Decoration is very modern and relaxing, chairs are also very comfortable!<br><br>The selections on the menu is a little limited, but I didn&#39;t mind that.  Specializes on what you are good at is key.  On two separate occasions, I tried the Chicken Pot Pie and the Mac and Cheese with Smoked Ham.  Both dishes were well-made!  Mac and Cheese was baked to perfection although it did feel a little heavy, the Chicken Pot Pie was full of ingredients and the puff layer to cover the pie was amazingly done!<br><br>For appetizer I tried the deep fried beer cheese &#34;rarebit&#34; and it was also very good.  You can really taste the beer and the honey mustard pairing complemented well with the beer cheese.<br><br>5 out of 5 in my book!  Very cozy and relaxing environment with great food!</p>

        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                
    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
            <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">

                <div class="review_tags">
                
        <span  class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i  class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite"></i> 1 check-in</span>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Make a reservation since it&#39;s a pretty busy restaurant and not very large. I had emailed to ask a question about the menu and place my reservation - they responded within hours.<br><br>The Mac And Cheese was deliciously creamy and filling. My husband had the Fried Haddock Po Boy which was tasty as well and came with a generous portion of fries. My dish was better though ;)<br><br>We were seated right next to the open kitchen which I thought was awesome at first. I quickly realized that there were some fall decorations (squash etc) on the booth separating my table and the kitchen, and they were attracting fruit flies. None came on my food and they weren&#39;t inside the actual kitchen area, but obviously this was off-putting.</p>

                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                
    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_3" title="3.0 star rating">
            <img alt="3.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3.0">
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-10-10">
        10/10/2015
    </span>

    </div>

        
                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">This is a bit of a throwback from about 6 months ago, but came across this place on Yelp again and I wanted to go back. Me and a friend decided to stop by at 5pm on a Tuesday night. The restaurant was relatively empty, but it turned out almost every table had reservations. No biggie, I actually don&#39;t mind sitting at the bar if I&#39;m only with one other person. <br><br>Like other reviews, the clientèle were mainly suits a couple of classy ladies. It was still quite a casual setting so don&#39;t feel inclined to come here with a top hat and monocle. <br><br>Me and my friend actually came here for drinks and a bit of food. <br><br>Beef Tartare (18) - it was good. Ingredients seemed to be fresh, although I felt like I could of gotten the same dish elsewhere. It wasn&#39;t mind blowing but it was good. <br><br>So then we got cocktails. They were bomb (or maybe that&#39;s the cocktails talking, getting all cocky) . <br><br>The Argyle (13) - you can taste the hit. But the sweetness hit you after, pretending like you were never drinking in the first place. <br><br>Classic Caesar (11) - biased. I love Caesars because they are life and this was pretty good. Of course I&#39;ve had better, but oh man I&#39;ve had much worse.<br><br>Hibiscus Royal (12) - my favourite from the list. It&#39;s so soft, not too sweet, not too bitter but like you&#39;re sitting in the meadows.. With a cocktail. <br><br>The Devereaux (14) - it was good! Not bad, but not really my favourite. <br><br>The service was also good. I feel like it was an all around good restaurant at a good location. Not really a place where I HAVE to have gone to, but it&#39;s good (as I&#39;ve said before) .</p>

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                
    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
            <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5.0">
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-11-23">
        11/23/2015
    </span>

    </div>

                <div class="review_tags">
                
        <span  class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i  class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite"></i> 1 check-in</span>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">I came here on a whim with my cousin in a Thursday night. It was pretty busy but they had a no show so we got seated right away. I loved the atmosphere inside. It was dimly lit and not very pretentious, especially for a place in the financial district. It definitely is a nice spot to take a date. The menu isn&#39;t insanely extensive but I&#39;m also a non seafood and pork eater. I got the mac and cheese of course and my cousin got the fried chicken sandwich. I also got a 5oz of the white cuvee which was very delicious and not overly sweet. <br>My mac and cheese was in a fairly good size ramkin dish. It was very hot and gooey and covered in breadcrumbs which is how i like it. I did still feel a bit hungry though. My cousin&#39;s burger was so yummy. Definitely not your kfc fried chicken! I would try that again. The fries had a rosemary flavoring to it and i could have had buckets of it to myself. Such a winner this place was. It isn&#39;t the cheapest but i think my money was well spent. I would come back!</p>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Wow! Wow! Wow! This is what I have to say about this place. All the food here was simply amazing. We went there for lunch but it seems dinner is pretty similar.<br><br>- For appetizer we had deviled eggs - the filling was amazing and plentiful<br>- The main dish as a fish that I can&#39;t really remember the name - it was the plate of the day. Impossible to describe how amazing it was. The skin was crispy and it included a mix of sauces that were out of this world<br>- I was by then super full but couldn&#39;t leave a place like this without trying their dessert - once again went for the dessert of the day, a chocolate pie with fresh whipped cream on top - super crispy tart base and chocolate that tasted like a wonderful mousse<br><br>If there is one place I&#39;ll go back to eat when in Toronto is this place... no doubts</p>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">I like that it&#39;s a new addition to a fairly monotone formulaic strip. I like that it&#39;s welcoming and warm and cozy. I like that the servers are grown up hipsters. I like that its got dim lighting and mismatched plates.<br><br>But that&#39;s about it. I don&#39;t really like the menu all that much and i don&#39;t really like the smell of deep fry oil wafting in the air.</p>

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                
    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_3" title="3.0 star rating">
            <img alt="3.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3.0">
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-10-29">
        10/29/2015
    </span>

    </div>

        
                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">It was packed when we got here! Thank god we made reservations! We got our appetizers and drinks pretty quickly, but our Main dishes took a really long time to come! It was really busy, but it would have been nice if the servers acknowledged the long wait time for our food. <br><br>Chicken pâté was amazing! My fave dish! <br><br>Devilled eggs -very creamy, but I found it too salty<br><br>Chicken sandwich - the chicken was deep fried and very good! Nicely spiced. <br><br>Fish taco - the wraps were dry, but the deep fried fish was nice and tender. The sauce was interesting. It seemed to have indian spices in it. This wasn&#39;t good in my opinion. Will pass on it next time.<br><br>Pork sandwich - not bad. Very tender. <br><br>Lemon pancotta - this was ok. Nothing special. <br><br>Overall, I would come back for the pâté and chicken sandwich, and to try their infamous Mac and cheese and chicken pot pie.</p>

            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                
    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
            <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4.0">
    </div>

            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-10-25">
        10/25/2015
    </span>

    </div>

        
                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Every time I lookup for a good place to grab dinner at downtown Toronto I always see The Gabardine popping up on Yelp. The reviews looked great, the food looked warm and hearty, so on a cold weekday night I dropped by this restaurant with a friend. This place is located right next to the 7-11 that I always go to for my usual fix of cheap XL coffee.<br><br>We ordered the Mac and Cheese with ham on top and the chicken pot pie, they each costed around $20. I was actually looking to order the chicken waffle but they no longer offer that :( Mac and Cheese was amazing. It was warm, creamy, and I liked crunchy burnt areas. Best Mac and Cheese I have ever tried. I liked the pastry crust of the chicken pot pie, however the soup was just alright...still bumped out not getting the chicken waffle boooo.<br><br>There was actually a time limit on your table of one and a half hour. We came at around 5:15 and were told we could stay until 6:30. It was quiet when we sat down and I could tell the restaurant getting busier as our time limit approaches. Eventually people had to wait for a table when we left. <br><br>Still can&#39;t get over the fact that chicken waffle is gone from their menu for good. Well guess it&#39;s time to try out other places</p>

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                
    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
            <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4.0">
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-09-19">
        9/19/2015
    </span>

    </div>

        
                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Visited The Gabardine for the first time while attending TIFF. It&#39;s got a great spot in the downtown core, although, unfortunately for them there is scaffolding covering the large windows into their well-decorated interior. <br><br>The food was all excellent. Every bite was filled with flavour, whether it was the crust of the chicken pot pie or the fries. The menu is very diverse with dishes from all corners of the world. Reflects Toronto well. The prices are very reasonable for its location.  The service was prompt, polite and professional. Reservations for dinner were easy to make and, most importantly, kept. The only downside I found was that drink prices, especially draft beers, were much higher than nearby establishments. <br><br>Would I go there again? Absolutely!</p> 
            
    </div>

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                
    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
            <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4.0">
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-08-26">
        8/26/2015
    </span>

    </div>

                <div class="review_tags">
                
        <span  class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i  class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite"></i> 1 check-in</span>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">I came here for brunch with some friends as party of 6. I feel like it&#39;s so hard nowadays to find a really good breakfast/lunch/brunch place in Toronto. I&#39;m so glad that I came across this place. Most of the meals we had eaten over the week were subpar or absolutely terrible, so it was nice to FINALLY have a good meal.<br><br>The restaurant is under construction around the exterior, so it can be a little difficult to find. If you need a landmark to get an idea of where the restaurant is, it is nearish to the Eaton Centre and Old City Hall. <br><br>The restaurant was very busy. The environment was casual, but the tables were very close to together. Be prepared to get cozy with your neighbours as there isn&#39;t a lot of room to move around in this place.<br><br>We were seated within minutes, and our orders were taken quite quickly. My friends ordered Mac &#39;n&#39; Cheese, while others ordered the Fish Tacos and the Sirloin Bacon Cheeseburger. They all enjoyed their meals. Looking back, my friends, who were visiting from all over Canada and the USA, did nothing but reminisce about how good the mac &#39;n&#39; cheese was, so much so that they started dreaming about it (literally). Oh boy, did that mac &#39;n&#39; cheese become a recurrent topic of discussion when recounting their vacation. <br><br>I ordered the Sirloin Bacon Cheeseburger. It was sooooooooooooo good. The burger patty completely cooked, but still maintained the taste. The burger as a whole was oozing with juicy goodness (4.5/5 in taste). <br><br>The portion size was large, and the food was very filling! The positive reviews about this place are true to their nature.</p>

        <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                
    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_3" title="3.0 star rating">
            <img alt="3.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3.0">
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-08-15">
        8/15/2015
    </span>

    </div>

                <div class="review_tags">
                
        <span  class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite-wrap review-tag"><i  class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_checkin_c-common_sprite"></i> 1 check-in</span>

        </div>

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">3.5 stars - we went here before heading to the Blue Jays game, it is super close to my work so very convenient (hard to spot though due to scaffolding). I made a reservation which was a good call as they were very busy when I got there.<br>The restaurant is small but cozy, trendy feel. The staff was very efficient and I guess you would have to be with that many people to serve! <br>I wasn&#39;t blown away by the food and I can speak for myself only right now. I got the Trinidadian Chana sandwich, I originally wanted the risotto but unfortunately for me that days special was with goat cheese, the worst cheese of all the cheeses! The sandwich was good, the coleslaw was yummy and the bun, though it looks unappealing, was actually great - toasty and buttery. The Chana was ok, I have def had better, all together it works. Fries were nice, really enjoyed the seasoning. I just felt like it was all good but not great. I got the hibiscus Royale to drink, it was really good and very potent, but also cost the same as my meal!<br>My boyfriend got the chicken pot pie. It was huge! The crust was fresh and perfectly done. The inside was very creamy and hot, I got the impression he felt it didn&#39;t have enough chicken in it. He did seem to enjoy it overall, I think with his meal the rating would have been higher.<br>I still really want to check out their Mac n Cheese, with seasoned bread crumbs on top. So I will likely be back and maybe that will up the rating!</p>

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
            <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Went tonight for my birthday dinner with some friends and it was hands down the best dinner I&#39;ve had in a long time!<br><br>We ordered deep fried beer cheese, soft corn tortillas, mac and cheese, and the chicken pot pie. We shared everything amongst the three of us, and everything was delicious. All menu items ordered were absolutely delicious and service was quick and friendly. I would highly recommend this restaurant.  <br><br>I do suggest calling a few days in advance to make reservations as the restaurant is small and it took us two days to get a hold of someone, but it was well worth the wait!</p>

    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_3" title="3.0 star rating">
            <img alt="3.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">

        8/7/2015

                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Been here several times, tried a few things on the menu.<br><br>Love the environment (this most recent time there were quite a few flies on the wall... minus a star for that...), dim, romantic, nicely decorated, attentive staff.<br><br>hubby absolutely loves the burger, it also comes with heaping plate of seasoned fries. I&#39;ve tried the mac and cheese with ham, the chicken pot pie, the fish tacos, as well as the fish sandwich. Maybe the fish sandwich was a meh - bun was a bit weird. But over all, The quality of food here is always awesome.<br><br>and certainly, it helps to have a nice cold beer with your burger. try it, and steer clear of the flies</p>

                <div class="review-content">
            <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
        <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                
    <div class="rating-very-large">
        <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
            <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84">
        </i>
            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4.0">
    </div>


        </div>
            <span class="rating-qualifier">
            <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-07-11">
        7/11/2015
    </span>

    </div>

        
                <p itemprop="description" lang="en">Holy cow is this place good. Fast and friendly service and amazing food. Boyfriend got the steak and fries, which he said was delicious and I got the zucchini and mint risotto (the risotto changes daily). We also ordered the beer cheese croquettes with the honey mustard dipping sauce - LIFE CHANGING. I would come here specifically for them. Loved the open kitchen concept because you could actually see the chefs making the food. Good tap list. The ambience was also nice. Location is not far from some attractions which is good because we were able to walk back to our hotel relatively quickly. Had to knock off a star because our server forgot we ordered the appetizer but quickly changed that and brought us one (sadly while we were eating our meal already though). Overall a great experience and would come back.</p> 
                        
        <ul class="photo-box-grid clearfix js-content-expandable lightbox-media-parent" data-ad-logging-csrf="5d602d325eebdc56aa0136698518a61a1ff705a1ab8e909b417fdddfe7acfd5d" data-ad-logging-uri="/ad_acknowledgment" data-dfp-attributes="[[&#34;category&#34;, [&#34;restaurant&#34;]], [&#34;city&#34;, &#34;Toronto&#34;], [&#34;attrrating&#34;, &#34;4.0&#34;], [&#34;bizid&#34;, &#34;hkZh4tAa2oJ34i8hxej6Zg&#34;], [&#34;language&#34;, &#34;en&#34;], [&#34;country&#34;, &#34;ca&#34;], [&#34;section&#34;, &#34;bizphotos&#34;], [&#34;scategory2&#34;, [&#34;newcanadia&#34;]], [&#34;dma_code&#34;, &#34;000&#34;], [&#34;zipcode&#34;, &#34;M5H 3W9&#34;], [&#34;sk&#34;, &#34;no&#34;], [&#34;signed_in&#34;, &#34;no&#34;], [&#34;mode&#34;, &#34;live&#34;]]" data-dfp-sizes="[[728, 90]]" data-dfp-type="biz" data-ga-path="media_lightbox/servlet:biz_details/type:biz" data-logging-csrf="0fefb21213ca2b685465de1462edd93f155895f4f73955833a1c949eb0dc53bf" data-logging-uri="/biz_photos/hkZh4tAa2oJ34i8hxej6Zg/log_views" data-media-count="2" data-media-url="/biz_photos/get_media_slice/hkZh4tAa2oJ34i8hxej6Zg?reviewid=rZU3cVNSEUq13_cFHmUSPQ" data-starting-index="0">
